like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . contact your doctor immediately if you have : - fever , signs of infection or extreme tiredness . these may be due to rare decrease of some blood cells . - difficulty in breathing or swallowing , which may be signs of nervous system problems : - confusion , disorientation , disorientation , confusion , disorientation , loss of consciousness , high blood pressure , changes in mental status , confusion , disorientation , disorientation , confusion , disorientation , loss of consciousness , high or low blood pressure , sudden shortness of breath or breathlessness , which may be signs of a serious condition called posterior reversible encephalopathy syndrome ( pres ). - if you experience a sudden decrease in blood pressure , which could make you feel faint or have difficulty breathing , as these may be signs of a serious condition called posterior reversible encephalopathy syndrome ( pres ). - if you experience a combination of fever , chills , lightheadedness , lightheadedness or loss of consciousness , as these may be signs of a serious condition called posterior reversible encephalopathy syndrome ( pres ). tell your doctor immediately if you develop a combination of any of these symptoms , as these may be signs of a serious condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . allergic reactions : anaphylaxis , swelling of the face , lips , tongue and / or throat , which may cause difficulty in breathing or swallowing , swelling of the face , lips , tongue and / or throat , which may cause difficulty in breathing or swallowing , drop in blood pressure , fast heartbeat and feeling of faintness , a general feeling of tiredness . these symptoms generally develop in a rapid fashion . these could be symptoms of a serious allergic reaction . common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) urinary tract infection common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) chest_infection ( awareness of your heart beat ) urinary tract infection , such as headache , dizziness , taste disturbance , cough stomach pain , abdominal pain , discomfort or discomfort in the ear , feeling of heaviness in the abdomen , or loosening of a tooth . these could be signs of bone damage in the ear . discomfort or pain in your abdomen , back or jaw , painful joints , back pain , pain in the abdomen , back or back , painful joints . very rare side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 , 000 people ) serious allergic reactions ( anaphylaxis ) have been reported in patients treated with anaphylaxis . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in nucala v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .

consciousness , confusion , hallucinations , changes in your mental status , confusion , hallucinations , loss of consciousness , severe bleeding in the stomach or bowels , yellowing of the skin and eyes ( jaundice ), dark coloured urine , extremities , dark coloured urine , or dark urine , aggressiveness or dark urine , aggressiveness or dark urine , or heavy menstrual periods . if you notice any of these , tell your doctor straight away . other side effects tell your doctor or pharmacist if you notice any of the following side effects : difficulty in breathing , weakness or itching ,
